***поперечный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поперечный.html>попере́чный</a> (10969)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">поперёк</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poperjók</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">across</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поперечный.html>попере́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poperéčnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>cross-
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поперечный.html>попере́чное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сечение.html>сече́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poperéčnoje</b> sečénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cross-section</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>transverse, crosswise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каждый.html>ка́ждый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встречный.html>встре́чный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поперечный.html>попере́чный</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">káždyj vstréčnyj i <b>poperéčnyj</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">any Tom, Dick or Harry, anyone</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">anyone oncoming or crosswise</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>lateral</li></ol>

***попечение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:попечение.html>попече́ние</a> (23333)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попечение.html>попече́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">popečénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попечение.html>попече́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попечение.html>попече́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попечение.html>попече́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>care
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ть</a> кого́-л <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:попечение.html>попече́нии</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">imétʹ kovó-l na <b>popečénii</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">have smb in charge; have smb to take care of; have smb to care for</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

***попивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:попивать.html>попива́ть</a> (15469)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попивать.html>попива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">popivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drink slowly, to sip
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиди́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чайка.html>чаёк</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:попивать.html>попива́ет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on tam sidít i čajók <b>popivájet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he sits there sipping his tea</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take to drink, to drink occasionally, to take to the bottle</li></ol>

***попирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:попирать.html>попира́ть</a> (25539)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-пира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-pirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попирать.html>попира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">popirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попрать.html>попра́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">lofty style</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to trample
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:попирать.html>попира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>popirátʹ</b> nogámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tread under foot</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to defy, to flout, to scorn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:попирать.html>попира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>права́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>popirátʹ</b> pravá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to violate the rights</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to violate</li></ol>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="переносное значение">перен.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:пренебрегать.html>пренебрега́я</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:грубый.html>гру́бо</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нарушать.html>наруша́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:унижать.html>унижа́ть</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

</ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пописать.html>пописа́ть</a> (21517)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пописать.html>пописа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">popisátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to write <i>(for some time, for a while)</i>, to do some writing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пописать.html>попи́шешь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ničevó ne popíšešʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nothing can be done about it; you can't help it</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to paint, to spend some time painting</li></ol>

***пописывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пописывать.html>попи́сывать</a> (29645)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пописывать.html>попи́сывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">popísyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to write <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">repeatedly or frequently</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/iterative_aspect" class="extiw" title="w:iterative aspect">iterative</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пописывать.html>попи́сывал</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:статейка.html>стате́йки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разный.html>ра́зных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бульварный.html>бульва́рных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:газетенка.html>газетёнках</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>popísyval</b> statéjki v ráznyx bulʹvárnyx gazetjónkax.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He <b>used to write</b> some little articles for some tabloids.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This is semantically an iterative verb, but unlike many such verbs it has a full conjugation in the standard language.</li></ul>

***поплавать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поплавать.html>попла́вать</a> (25039)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавать.html>пла́вать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plávatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поплавать.html>попла́вать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poplávatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавать.html>пла́вать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to swim for a while, to float for a while
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поплавать.html>попла́вала</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:озеро.html>о́зере</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пошла́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:домой.html>домо́й</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná <b>poplávala</b> v ózere i pošlá domój.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">She swam in the lake for a while and went home.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to sail for a while</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This is an abstract verb. Its concrete counterpart is <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поплыть.html>поплы́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poplýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поплакать.html>попла́кавший</a> (11902)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поплакать.html>попла́кавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poplákavšij</span>)
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поплевать.html>поплева́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poplevávšij</span>)

***поплевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поплевать.html>поплева́ть</a> (20806)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плевать.html>плева́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поплевать.html>поплева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poplevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spit several times</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spit for awhile</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поплыть.html>поплы́ть</a> (4478)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плыть.html>плыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поплыть.html>поплы́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poplýtʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плыть.html>плыть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to start swimming, to start floating
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поплыть.html>поплы́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́рону</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:маяк.html>маяка́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>poplýl</b> v stóronu majaká.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He started swimming towards the lighthouse.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to start sailing</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This is a concrete verb. Its abstract counterpart is <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поплавать.html>попла́вать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poplávatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

***поползновение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поползновение.html>поползнове́ние</a> (25422)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поползти.html>поползти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">popolztí</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to crawl</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + an unclear infix + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поползновение.html>поползнове́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">popolznovénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поползновение.html>поползнове́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поползновение.html>поползнове́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поползновение.html>поползнове́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> inclination, impulse</li>
<li>feeble effort</li></ol>

***поползти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поползти.html>поползти́</a> (4232)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ползти.html>ползти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поползти.html>поползти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">popolztí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ползти.html>ползти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to (start) creeping, crawling</li>
<li>to start moving slowly</li>
<li>to start spreading <i>(of rumours)</i></li>
<li>to start fraying, ravelling out <i>(of fabric)</i></li>
<li>to start slipping, collapsing <i>(of soil)</i></li></ol>

***пополнение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пополнение.html>пополне́ние</a> (11266)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пополнить.html>попо́лнить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">popólnitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пополнение.html>пополне́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">popolnénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пополнение.html>пополне́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пополнение.html>пополне́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пополнение.html>пополне́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>replenishment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пополнение.html>пополне́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:запас.html>запа́сов</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:топливо.html>то́плива</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>popolnénije</b> zapásov tópliva</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">refuelling</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пополнение.html>пополне́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:библиотека.html>библиоте́ки</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>popolnénije</b> bibliotéki</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">stocking of library funds</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пополнение.html>пополне́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:боеприпас.html>боеприпа́сами</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>popolnénije</b> bojepripásami</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">replenishment of ammunition</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> reinforcement, fresh forces, additional staff
